---

## 1. Purpose and scope

**v1.5** bridges governed substrate work (closed **v1** arc **M00–M61**, post-v1 phases **PV1**, **PX1**, **PX2**) and a potential **v2** recharter. It exists to run a **serious long local GPU training campaign** with **merge-grade or operator-approved provenance**, and to produce a **bounded, replay-native, explainable** Terran-first 1v1 agent—**without** overclaiming ladder universality, global benchmark superiority, or v2 readiness.

**In scope for the v1.5 program (not necessarily for every milestone):**

- Long GPU training with manifests, checkpoint lineage, eval cadence, and receipts.
- Strong-agent evaluation under **predeclared** benchmark ladders.
- Replay-native **XAI** evidence packs on frozen contracts.
- Optional **human-panel** or bounded “beats most humans” claims **only** under frozen protocol and recorded non-claims.

**Out of scope for governance documents:** executing training in CI by default; claiming results that operators have not produced under declared protocols.

---

## 2. Relationship to prior phases

| Phase | Role relative to v1.5 |
| --- | --- |
| **v1 (M00–M61)** | Delivered governed replay-native SC2 substrate, deterministic artifact families, bounded training/eval surfaces. Remains the technical foundation. |
| **PV1** | Long industrial campaign discipline and operator-local scaling evidence—not autonomous full-game strength as v1.5’s sole gate. |
| **PX1** | Full industrial run + demo proof packaging—separate from autonomous skill development. |
| **PX2 (M00–M03)** | **Closed / transition-complete.** Delivered bounded self-play and operator-local surfaces; **did not** ship a long wall-clock GPU training session as a program deliverable. |

---

## 3. Moonshot goals (five pillars)

Success of the **overall** v1.5 program requires evidence for all five (see moonshot doc for detail). **V15-M00** only **defines** these—it does not satisfy them.

1. **Full GPU training run completed** — manifests, lineage, logs, receipts (not a smoke or fixture-only story).
2. **Strong-agent benchmark passed** — predeclared ladder (fixture → scripted → heuristic → prior checkpoints → live → human panel as applicable).
3. **Replay-native XAI demonstration** — frozen artifact shapes; wins, losses, macro/tactical/scout/counterfactual coverage.
4. **Human-benchmark claim bounded** — “beats most humans” only under declared STARLAB benchmark rules and non-claims.
5. **v2 go/no-go decision evidence-based** — proceed, harden, extend training, or recharter based on artifacts.

---

## 4. Standing non-claims (v1.5)

Unless separately proved and scoped:

- Not a global StarCraft II solution; not ladder dominance; not multi-race generality.
- Not guaranteed benchmark universality or replay↔execution equivalence.
- Not v2 by default; not **PX2-M04** auto-opened.
- XAI artifacts are **governed explanation packs**, not proofs of causal human-like reasoning.

**M00 non-claims:** No long GPU run completed in M00; no strong-agent, human-panel, or XAI completion claimed.

**M01 non-claims (persist after M01 closure):** No long GPU run; no **M01** environment lock surface (delivered in **M02**); no checkpoint lineage **runtime**; no XAI contract freeze or XAI execution; no benchmark execution; no human-panel execution; no v2; no **PX2-M04** / **PX2-M05**; no claim-critical asset rows in public registers (templates only). Milestone closure records merge/CI evidence only — **not** asset approval for claim-critical use.

**M02 non-claims (after M02 closure on `main` until superseded by later milestones):** V15-M02 defines and emits the long GPU run **environment-lock surface** and may normalize **supplied** operator probe JSON **or** run the **fixture** profile in CI. **Fixture `fixture_ci` output does not imply operator-local readiness** (including RTX 5090–class). It does **not** execute GPU training; does **not** run GPU shakedown (**V15-M07**); does **not** grant **long_run** or program long-GPU **authorization**; does **not** alone satisfy Gate B for a program-valid long run; does **not** claim operator-local hardware readiness from CI fixture output; does **not** run SC2, `nvidia-smi`, or map introspection in CI; does **not** implement checkpoint lineage **runtime**; does **not** freeze XAI; does **not** run benchmarks, human panel, or XAI execution; does **not** approve claim-critical real assets; does **not** open v2 or **PX2-M04** / **PX2-M05**. The field `long_gpu_run_authorized` in the M02 contract remains **false** — M02 does not grant program authorization.

**M03 non-claims (after M03 closure on `main` until superseded by later milestones as applicable):** V15-M03 defines and emits the **checkpoint lineage and resume-discipline** manifest (`starlab.v15.checkpoint_lineage_manifest.v1`). It is **metadata and governance only**: it may normalize operator-declared **lineage JSON** and may bind an **M02** environment lock file by **canonical JSON SHA-256**; it does **not** read or hash on-disk **checkpoint weight blobs**; does **not** verify checkpoint bytes by default; does **not** execute **trainer** resume or rollback; does **not** set `resume_execution_verified` / `rollback_execution_verified` to true at the program-manifest root (M03 does not prove execution); does **not** run GPU training or shakedown; does **not** authorize a long GPU run (`long_gpu_run_authorized` remains **false**); does **not** promote a “strong” checkpoint; does **not** approve real assets for claim-critical public registers; does **not** open v2 or **PX2-M04** / **PX2-M05**. A lineage manifest is **not** proof that checkpoint bytes exist unless `hash_verification_status` and external scope say so. A **resume receipt** is **not** proof that training resumed unless an external path says so, and M03 does not independently verify that path.

**M04 non-claims (after M04 closure on `main` until superseded by later milestones as applicable):** V15-M04 defines and emits the **XAI evidence contract** (`starlab.v15.xai_evidence_pack.v1`) and **fixture** `v15_xai_evidence_pack.json` + report. It is **metadata and schema only**: it may validate operator-declared **evidence JSON** and redact path-like strings; it does **not** run model **inference**; does **not** generate real saliency, attribution, or concept activations; does **not** execute counterfactual **evaluation**; does **not** parse real **replays**; does **not** read checkpoint **blobs**; does **not** verify checkpoint **bytes** as an execution path; does **not** **prove** explanation **faithfulness**; does **not** run **benchmarks** or **human** evaluation; does **not** execute GPU **training** or **shakedown**; does **not** set `long_gpu_run_authorized` to **true**; does **not** approve real XAI assets for claim-critical public **registers**; does **not** open **v2** or **PX2-M04** / **PX2-M05**. A fixture pack is **not** an explanation of a trained agent. Public **`docs/xai_evidence_register.md`** gets **no** new real XAI **rows** in M04 (contract definition only).

**M05 non-claims (during and after M05; supersede only where a later milestone explicitly changes posture):** V15-M05 defines and emits the **strong-agent benchmark protocol and scorecard contract** (`starlab.v15.strong_agent_scorecard.v1` with `protocol_profile_id` `starlab.v15.strong_agent_benchmark_protocol.v1`) and **fixture** `v15_strong_agent_scorecard.json` + report. It is **metadata and protocol vocabulary only** (ladder, scorecard field definitions, gate shapes, evidence classes, reserved human-panel and XAI-review milestones): it may validate **fixture** protocol metadata and may normalize **operator-declared** protocol JSON (with absolute-path **redaction**); it does **not** run **benchmarks** or tournaments; does **not** run **live SC2**; does **not** **evaluate** a **checkpoint**; does **not** **select** or **promote** a “strong” agent; does **not** run **XAI review** or **human-panel** execution; does **not** add **real** match or scorecard **results**; does **not** execute GPU **training** or **shakedown**; does **not** set `long_gpu_run_authorized` / `strong_agent_claim_authorized` / `benchmark_execution_performed` to **true**; does **not** approve real assets for **claim-critical** public **registers**; does **not** open **v2** or **PX2-M04** / **PX2-M05**. A **strong-agent scorecard contract** is **not** evidence that a strong-agent benchmark has **passed**. A **fixture** benchmark protocol is **schema / wiring** evidence only, **not** a performance result.

**M06 non-claims (during and after M06; supersede only where a later milestone explicitly changes posture):** V15-M06 defines and emits the human-panel benchmark protocol contract (`starlab.v15.human_panel_benchmark.v1` with `protocol_profile_id` `starlab.v15.human_panel_benchmark_protocol.v1`) and **fixture** `v15_human_panel_benchmark.json` + `v15_human_panel_benchmark_report.json`. It is **protocol and governance metadata only**: it does **not** recruit or evaluate human participants; does **not** run human-panel **matches**; does **not** run live **SC2**; does **not** evaluate or **promote** a **checkpoint**; does **not** add real participant **identities** or **results**; does **not** authorize a “beats most humans” **claim**; does **not** run GPU **training** or **shakedown**; does **not** perform **XAI** **review**; does **not** set `human_benchmark_claim_authorized`, `strong_agent_claim_authorized`, `benchmark_execution_performed`, `human_panel_execution_performed`, or `long_gpu_run_authorized` to **true**; does **not** approve real assets for **claim-critical** public **registers**; does **not** open **v2** or **PX2-M04** / **PX2-M05**. A **human-panel benchmark protocol** is **not** evidence that a human benchmark has been **run** or **passed**. **Public** `docs/human_benchmark_register.md` receives **no** new real participant **rows** in M06 (one-line M06 **note** only; **no rows** in the public register table). 

**M07 non-claims (during and after M07; supersede only where a later milestone explicitly changes posture):** V15-M07 defines and emits the training smoke / short GPU shakedown receipt contract (`starlab.v15.training_run_receipt.v1` with profile `starlab.v15.training_smoke_short_gpu_shakedown.v1`) and may run a bounded **operator-local** GPU or CPU shakedown only when **explicitly** invoked with `--allow-operator-local-execution`. It does **not** execute the **V15-M08** long GPU campaign; does **not** authorize a long run; does **not** promote a checkpoint; does **not** run a strong-agent benchmark; does **not** run human-panel matches; does **not** perform XAI review; does **not** authorize human-benchmark or strong-agent claims; does **not** approve real public register rows for claim-critical use; does **not** commit model weights or checkpoint blobs; and does **not** open v2 or PX2-M04/PX2-M05. A short GPU shakedown receipt is **not** evidence that the long GPU campaign has completed or that a strong agent exists. **M07** may close as **shakedown tooling and receipt contract implemented** if no operator-local GPU is available; **M07** must **not** be described as “operator-local GPU shakedown **completed**” unless a real private receipt exists.

**M08 non-claims block:** V15-M08 defines and, when explicitly authorized, executes the long GPU campaign under `starlab.v15.long_gpu_training_manifest.v1` and related training-run receipt surfaces. M08 may record that a long GPU run was authorized, executed, and completed within a declared operator-local scope only if the preflight gates pass and a real campaign receipt exists. M08 does not by itself promote a checkpoint; does not pass or execute the strong-agent benchmark; does not run human-panel matches; does not perform XAI review; does not authorize human-benchmark or strong-agent claims; does not approve v2; does not prove ladder dominance, global SC2 solution, multi-race generality, benchmark universality, or replay↔execution equivalence; does not commit raw checkpoints, model weights, replays, logs, or private operator paths; and does not open PX2-M04/PX2-M05. A completed long GPU campaign is training evidence, not a strong-agent claim.

**M09 non-claims block:** V15-M09 defines and emits checkpoint evaluation and promotion-decision artifacts under `starlab.v15.checkpoint_evaluation.v1` and `starlab.v15.checkpoint_promotion_decision.v1`. **Default and fixture / honest public paths** remain **`blocked_missing_m08_campaign_receipt`** / not promoted; **all** program claim flags stay **false** on those paths. A hypothetical `promoted_candidate_for_downstream_evaluation` label, if ever emitted under explicit non-default evidence, is **governance routing only** — **not** “strong agent,” “release-ready,” or a benchmark pass. M09 does not execute the long GPU campaign; does not train new checkpoints; does not pass or execute the strong-agent benchmark; does not authorize strong-agent or human-benchmark claims; does not run human-panel matches; does not perform XAI review; does not release model weights; does not approve v2; does not prove ladder dominance, global SC2 solution, multi-race generality, benchmark universality, or replay↔execution equivalence; and does not commit raw checkpoints, model weights, replays, logs, or private operator paths. A checkpoint promotion decision record is **governance metadata** for routing labels, not a strong-agent or performance claim.

**M10 non-claims block (closed on `main` — PR #136; non-claims and default blocked/fixture posture remain in force):** V15-M10 defines and emits the replay-native XAI **demonstration and reporting** surface under `starlab.v15.replay_native_xai_demonstration.v1` and binds M04 `starlab.v15.xai_evidence_pack.v1` and M09 `starlab.v15.checkpoint_promotion_decision.v1` JSON by **canonical SHA-256** when operator inputs are supplied. It emits `v15_replay_native_xai_demonstration.json`, a JSON report, and a deterministic **`v15_xai_explanation_report.md`**. M10 does **not** run model **inference**; does **not** parse raw **replays**; does **not** read checkpoint **weight blobs**; does **not** **prove** explanation **faithfulness**; does **not** run human-panel or strong-agent **benchmarks**; does **not** authorize ladder, v2, or human-benchmark **claims** by default; does **not** add **claim-critical** public XAI **rows** in **`docs/xai_evidence_register.md`** on the default path; and does **not** commit **raw** media, saliency tensors, or **private** operator paths. A stronger demonstration label is allowed only with explicit non-default operator evidence; fixture and default CI remain **schema/report validation** only.

**M11 non-claims block (closed on `main` — PR #137; default fixture / honest public paths):** V15-M11 defines the human-panel **execution evidence** and **bounded human-benchmark claim-decision** surfaces under **`starlab.v15.human_panel_execution.v1`** and **`starlab.v15.human_benchmark_claim_decision.v1`**, binding M06 / M09 / M10 JSON by **canonical SHA-256** when operator inputs are supplied (preflight additionally binds M08 / M05 / M03). M11 does **not** recruit human participants; does **not** run human-panel **matches** in CI; does **not** run live **SC2** by default; does **not** **promote** a **checkpoint**; does **not** **train** a **checkpoint**; does **not** prove a **strong-agent** benchmark; does **not** authorize “beats most humans,” ladder, strong-agent, or v2 **claims** on the default path; and does **not** commit participant identities, raw replays, videos, checkpoint blobs, weights, private operator paths, or private human-panel **notes**. The claim-decision artifact is a deterministic read of the execution artifact, not a second upstream binder. **No** **claim-critical** public human-benchmark **register** **rows** on the default path.

**M12 non-claims block (closed on `main` — PR #138; default fixture / honest public paths):** V15-M12 defines the **showcase agent release-pack governance surface** under **`starlab.v15.showcase_agent_release_pack.v1`**. It binds M08 campaign receipt, M09 promotion decision, M10 replay-native XAI demonstration, M11 human-benchmark claim decision, M05 strong-agent scorecard, and M03 checkpoint lineage JSON by **canonical SHA-256** when operator inputs are supplied. V15-M12 does not train a checkpoint; does not promote a checkpoint; does not execute a long GPU campaign; does not run strong-agent benchmarks; does not run live SC2; does not run XAI inference; does not run human-panel matches; does not authorize showcase-agent, strong-agent, human-benchmark, ladder, or v2 claims on the default path; and does not commit model weights, checkpoint blobs, raw replays, videos, saliency tensors, participant records, private operator notes, or private paths. **No** **claim-critical** public register **rows** on the default path. **v2** go/no-go remains **V15-M13**.

**M13 non-claims block (implementation / default fixture / honest public paths):** V15-M13 defines the **v2 go / no-go decision surface** under **`starlab.v15.v2_go_no_go_decision.v1`**. It binds the **M12** showcase release-pack JSON by **canonical SHA-256** and may optionally cross-check upstream M03/M05/M08/M09/M10/M11 JSON files against M12 `upstream_bindings`. V15-M13 does not train a checkpoint; does not promote a checkpoint; does not execute a long GPU campaign; does not run benchmarks; does not run live SC2; does not run XAI inference; does not run human-panel matches; does not release a showcase agent; does not authorize v2 on the default path; and does not commit model weights, checkpoint blobs, raw replays, videos, saliency tensors, participant records, private operator notes, or private paths. **No** **claim-critical** public register **rows** are added by default. Optional operator-declared evidence uses **`starlab.v15.v2_decision_operator_evidence_declared.v1`** (metadata-only; redacted on emit).

**M14 non-claims block (closed on `main` — PR #140; default fixture / honest public paths; non-claims remain in force):** V15-M14 defines evidence remediation and **operator evidence acquisition *readiness*** under **`starlab.v15.evidence_remediation_plan.v1`**. It does not execute a long GPU campaign; does not run a short GPU shakedown; does not train or promote a checkpoint; does not run benchmarks; does not run live SC2; does not run XAI inference; does not run human-panel matches; does not release a showcase agent; does not authorize v2; does not collect or certify new replay, data, model weight, human-panel, video, or XAI assets; and does not commit raw weights, checkpoints, replays, videos, saliency tensors, participant records, private operator notes, or private paths. Proposed follow-on milestones **V15-M15**–**V15-M21** are **roadmap labels only** until separately approved and implemented; they are **not** evidence that operator work has completed or that claim-critical register rows are cleared.

**M15 non-claims block (closed on `main` — PR #141; preflight only):** V15-M15 defines the **operator evidence collection preflight** surface under **`starlab.v15.operator_evidence_collection_preflight.v1`**. It does **not** collect operator evidence; does **not** run a long GPU campaign, short GPU shakedown, live SC2, benchmark matches, XAI inference, or human-panel execution; does **not** train or promote a checkpoint; does **not** release a showcase agent; does **not** authorize v2 or v2 recharter; and does **not** add claim-critical public register **rows** or clear rights for private assets. **V15-M16**–**V15-M21** are **sequencing targets** in the preflight map only, **not** completed evidence. Fixture/default CI is **wiring and vocabulary**; optional JSON bindings are **SHA-only**; **M15** **does not** assert that M13/M14 file bindings represent collected operator work unless supplied by the operator and validated under separate milestones.

**M16 non-claims block (closed on `main` — PR #142; default fixture / honest operator-local paths):** V15-M16 defines the **short GPU / environment evidence** surface under **`starlab.v15.short_gpu_environment_evidence.v1`**. It does **not** execute the **full** long GPU campaign; does **not** set **`long_gpu_run_authorized`** to **true**; does **not** train or promote a checkpoint; does **not** run live SC2, benchmark matches, XAI inference, or human-panel execution; does **not** release a showcase agent; does **not** authorize v2 or v2 recharter; does **not** add claim-critical public register **rows** by default; and does **not** commit raw weights, checkpoints, replays, videos, saliency tensors, or private operator paths. Optional **M02** / **M07** / **M08** / **M15** JSON bindings are **SHA-only** metadata; **M08** remains manifest / preflight **tooling** unless paired with valid operator campaign receipts. **`m17_opening_recommendation`** is **planning / opening posture only**; **M17** owns long GPU campaign evidence.

**M17 non-claims block (closed on `main` — PR #143; default fixture / honest public paths; non-claims remain in force):** V15-M17 defines the **long GPU campaign evidence / preflight** surface under **`starlab.v15.long_gpu_campaign_evidence.v1`**. It does **not** by itself authorize **`long_gpu_run_authorized: true`** on the default public fixture path; does **not** run GPU training in CI; does **not** train or **promote** a checkpoint; does **not** run strong-agent benchmarks, human-panel runs, or XAI inference; does **not** release a showcase agent; does **not** authorize v2 or v2 recharter; does **not** add claim-critical public register **rows** by default; and does **not** commit **raw** weights, checkpoints, replays, videos, **logs**, or **private** operator **paths**. Operator-local **M16** JSON is validated by **content**; public code does **not** hardcode a private operator M16 file SHA. Real long GPU **execution** uses **M08** **`run_v15_long_gpu_campaign`** with explicit guards and honest receipts; **M18** owns candidate checkpoint **evaluation readiness / refusal** metadata (inputs for a **future** evaluation milestone; **not** evaluation execution).

**M18 non-claims block:** V15-M18 defines **`starlab.v15.checkpoint_evaluation_readiness.v1`** — deterministic **readiness / refusal** classification only. It does **not** execute checkpoint evaluation or measure strength; does **not** promote a checkpoint; does **not** run long GPU training, live SC2, M08/M50 campaign execution, or benchmark matches; does **not** authorize human-panel, XAI, showcase, or v2 claims; does **not** treat watchability-only evidence or **`.joblib`** harness bundles as promoted **PyTorch** checkpoints; does **not** infer meaningful training checkpoints from **`not_executed`** receipts or **`checkpoint_count: 0`**; does **not** commit **`out/**`**, raw weights, checkpoints, or private operator paths.

**M19 non-claims block:** V15-M19 defines **`starlab.v15.candidate_checkpoint_evaluation_package.v1`** — **assembly, binding, and consistency** only. It does **not** run strong-agent or human benchmarks; does **not** execute checkpoint evaluation, live SC2, or measure strength; does **not** promote a checkpoint; does **not** read or hash on-disk **checkpoint weight blobs**; does **not** treat **`evaluation_package_ready`** as a benchmark pass — that status is **`ready_for_future_checkpoint_evaluation` only**; keeps **`strength_evaluated`**, **`checkpoint_promoted`**, **`benchmark_passed`**, **`xai_claim_authorized`**, **`human_benchmark_claim_authorized`**, **`showcase_release_authorized`**, and **`v2_authorized`** **false** in the public record; does **not** add claim-critical public register **rows**; does **not** open **M20** / **M21** XAI, human, or v2 primary tracks from assembly alone. **`operator_declared`** is **metadata-only** (normalize / validate / path redaction) — **no** blob I/O, **no** training, **no** evaluation. Wrong **`--m18-readiness-json`** **contract_id** is **`blocked_invalid_candidate_package`**.

**M21 non-claims block:** V15-M21 defines **`starlab.v15.operator_t1_30min_gpu_run_execution.v1`** — operator-local **T1** execution **evidence framing** only (distinct filenames from **M20** gate JSON). It delegates governed training orchestration to **`run_v15_t1_30min_candidate_checkpoint_gate`** — **no** duplicate training stack; **no** merge CI GPU execution by default (fixture **`t1_30min_run_not_started`** / honest blocker statuses); does **not** evaluate strength or promote checkpoints; does **not** run benchmark tournaments, live SC2, XAI inference, human-panel execution, showcase release, or authorize **v2**; does **not** execute **T2**/**T3** tiers; keeps enumerated **`non_claims`** aligned with **M20** on honest paths; **does not** commit **`out/**`**, checkpoints, logs, replays, videos, or unsanitized paths.

**M22 non-claims block:** V15-M22 is the **real operator attempt** milestone for the **M21** runner path. On honest paths it **does not** authorize strength claims, checkpoint promotion, benchmark passes, XAI or human-panel execution, showcase release, **v2**, **T2**, or **T3**. A **`torch_cuda_unavailable`** (or equivalent) preflight block is **evidence of remediation need**, not a training outcome.

**M23 non-claims block:** V15-M23 is **operator environment remediation** — CUDA-capable **PyTorch** + **venv** alignment and honest **`torch.cuda.is_available()`** / GPU visibility checks. It **does not** claim the **T1** run **completed**, **does not** produce or promote checkpoints, **does not** evaluate strength, **does not** pass benchmarks, **does not** execute XAI or human-panel work, **does not** release showcase agents, **does not** authorize **v2**, and **does not** execute **T2**/**T3** unless separately chartered.

**M24 non-claims block:** V15-M24 is the **operator attempt** to rerun **M21** dry-run preflight under **`.venv`** and enter real **T1** only if preflight passes. On the recorded **blocked** path it **does not** claim **M21** preflight **passed**, **does not** claim **T1** **execution**, **does not** produce or promote checkpoints, **does not** evaluate strength, **does not** pass benchmarks, **does not** execute XAI or human-panel work, **does not** release showcase agents, **does not** authorize **v2**, and **does not** execute **T2**/**T3**. A **`missing_private_manifest_inputs`** classification is **input inventory evidence**, not a training outcome.

**M25 non-claims block:** V15-M25 is **manifest alignment and M21 dry-run preflight only**. It **does not** claim **real T1** GPU training **execution**; **does not** produce or promote a **candidate checkpoint**; **does not** evaluate strength; **does not** pass or execute benchmarks; **does not** execute XAI or human-panel work; **does not** release showcase agents; **does not** authorize **v2**; **does not** execute **T2**/**T3**. A green **M21** **`--dry-run-preflight-only`** run is **governed input validation**, not a training result. **Fixture**-mode **M15** preflight JSON (**`fixture_ci`**, **`operator_evidence_collection_status`:** **`not_started`**) is **preflight/sequencing**, not “operator evidence collected.”

**M26 non-claims block:** V15-M26 is the **real non-dry-run T1 attempt** after **M25** manifest alignment — **not** dry-run-only closeout. It **does not** equate **synthetic CUDA** checkpoint production with **meaningful SC2 agent training** or a **material SC2-backed training/rollout** workload; **does not** promote a **candidate checkpoint** (including when **`t1_30min_checkpoint_produced_package_ready`** or a hash-recorded **`.pt`** exists — **candidate only**); **does not** treat **`t1_30min_run_completed_no_checkpoint`** as strength evidence; **does not** pass or execute strong-agent benchmarks; **does not** execute XAI or human-panel work; **does not** release showcase agents; **does not** authorize **v2**; **does not** execute **T2**/**T3** unless separately chartered. **`t1_30min_completed_without_candidate_checkpoint`** is an **operator-local execution posture / packaging outcome** (Attempt A / pass1b-only), **not** a benchmark pass. Optional **`sc2-harness`** (`pip install -e ".[sc2-harness]"`) is **operator-local** for **`local_live_sc2`** paths and **not** implied by default CI fixture posture.

**M27 non-claims block:** V15-M27 is **SC2 rollout observability + training-path integration evidence** — **not** a substitute for long GPU **SC2** imitation/RL programs, **not** strength evaluation, **not** benchmark execution, **not** checkpoint promotion, **not** XAI, **not** human-panel execution, **not** showcase release, **not** **v2** / **T2**/**T3** authorization. Fixture mode (**`sc2_rollout_fixture_only`**) is **not** live **SC2**. The **integration-smoke** PyTorch step is **`integration_smoke_not_meaningful_learning`** — **not** a claim of policy improvement. **`v15_m27_nontrivial_macro_smoke_policy_v1`** reuses the **PX1 watchability** scaffold — **not** a new learned policy.

**M28 non-claims block:** V15-M28 is **SC2 rollout JSON → feature-conditioned bounded candidate training receipts** — **not** strength evaluation, **not** benchmark execution, **not** checkpoint promotion, **not** proof that **SC2-backed** training beats synthetic-only plumbing as gameplay skill, **not** XAI / human-panel / showcase / **v2** / **T2**/**T3** authorization. **`sc2_rollout_feature_conditioned_training_smoke_not_strength_learning`** — **not** “meaningful learning” unless separately evidenced. Fixture **`fixture_only`** is **not** operator-local M27 consumption on disk. Candidate **`.pt`** artifacts are **candidate only** — **hashed**, **not promoted**.

**M29 non-claims block:** V15-M29 targets **proof of full-wall-clock execution** (**~30 minutes**) for the **same SC2 rollout–conditioned bounded candidate-training path**, **without** asserting strength evaluation, benchmark pass, checkpoint promotion (candidate **`.pt`** hashes only), XAI inference, human-panel execution, showcase release, **v2**, **long GPU campaign**, **or** gameplay skill beyond controlled wiring receipts. Fixture **`--fixture-only-m29`** is **bounded seconds-scale** CI wiring — **not** the operator horizon. **`sc2_backed_t1_full_30min_completed_*`** classifications require **`observed_wall_clock_seconds`** near **≥ 1800s** (**±bounded tolerance**) — **early-stop-only** runs **cannot** authorize full-horizon closeout semantics.

**M30 non-claims block:** V15-M30 emits **`starlab.v15.candidate_checkpoint_evaluation_package.v1`** under **`package_profile_id`** **`starlab.v15.m30.sc2_backed_candidate_checkpoint_evaluation_package.v1`** by binding sealed **M27**/**M28**/**M29** JSON (**SHA consistency / assembly only**). It does **not** evaluate strength; does **not** pass or execute benchmarks; does **not** promote checkpoints; does **not** execute XAI; does **not** execute human-panel evaluation; does **not** release showcase agents; does **not** authorize **v2** or **T2**/**T3**. **`evaluation_package_ready`** means **`ready_for_future_checkpoint_evaluation`** only (honest package posture — **not** a benchmark result). Optional **`--m05-scorecard-json`** binds **`starlab.v15.strong_agent_scorecard.v1`** evaluation-protocol metadata **when supplied** — omission does **not** block readiness. **`upstream_m27_rollout.resolved_path`** absolute paths are **not** copied verbatim into public-facing package JSON (**redacted digest** instead).

Contracts: **`starlab.v15.candidate_live_adapter_spike.v1`**, **`starlab.v15.m52a.candidate_to_live_policy_adapter_spike.v1`**; **`python -m starlab.v15.emit_v15_m52_candidate_live_adapter_spike`**; **`python -m starlab.v15.run_v15_m52_candidate_live_adapter_spike`**; **`docs/runtime/v15_candidate_live_adapter_spike_v1.md`**.

A completed M53 run is training execution evidence only. **V15-M53** does not execute benchmark matches; does not emit benchmark pass/fail; does not evaluate strength; does not promote checkpoints; does not run XAI or human-panel evaluation; does not release a showcase agent; does not authorize v2; and does not execute T2–T5. Candidate checkpoints remain candidate-only unless a later promotion milestone says otherwise. **Strongest allowed claim (M55):** A declared evaluation package can be structurally preflighted for a later bounded readout, with deterministic refusal reasons and **claim_flags** held **false**.

**Standing M55 denials:** No evaluation execution. No benchmark pass/fail. No candidate promotion. No strong-agent claim. No human-panel claim. No XAI completion. No **v2** readiness claim. No **`torch.load`**. No checkpoint blob loading. No live SC2. No GPU inference. No **T2–T5** execution.

**V15-M56 closed:** **V15-M56** — *Bounded Evaluation Package Readout / Decision* — **closed** on `main` ([PR #196](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/196); merge **`478f56f18e8fdd2e6c415b9ab288804d52c496e0`**; **final PR-head SHA** **`2cac81386b7bf46214672f87d7d06445a6f2cd6e`**; **authoritative PR-head CI** [`25266981322`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25266981322) — **success**; **superseded PR-head CI:** [`25266845811`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25266845811) — **failure** (coverage gate on early head; superseded); **merge-boundary `main` CI** [`25267074715`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25267074715) — **success**); **merge method:** GitHub **merge commit**. **Implementation + fixture/governance CI closed.** **Runtime:** **`docs/runtime/v15_bounded_evaluation_package_readout_decision_v1.md`**. **Contracts:** **`starlab.v15.bounded_evaluation_package_readout_decision.v1`**, **`starlab.v15.bounded_evaluation_package_readout_decision_report.v1`**, **`starlab.v15.m56.bounded_evaluation_package_readout_decision.v1`**. **Immediate upstream:** sealed **§V15-M55** preflight JSON; **strict** `artifact_sha256` seal verification. **M56A** optional / non-gating. **Cross-check anchors:** M54 package **`bbe08673aa85beb0ae7e51a627a68c67fd95a930176d174d2c60bb96e4a278d6`**, M53 artifact **`18a1e6c39bb372c3f7edc595919963d12442467a74dd329e56f7cf0d0c816ec8`**, candidate **`7c91a4b7cec6b14d160c00bec768c4fb3199bd8bf0228b2436bd7fbc5dc6ea90`**. **Route:** **`route_to_future_governed_evaluation_design_or_execution_gate`** · **`recommended_not_executed`**. **Strongest allowed:** V15-M56 can read sealed V15-M55 preflight artifacts and emit a bounded readout / decision indicating whether the package is ready, blocked, or requires remediation for a future governed evaluation step. It does not execute evaluation or authorize benchmark/pass/promotion claims.

**Standing M56 non-claims:** No benchmark execution. No benchmark pass/fail. No scorecard results. No strength evaluation. No checkpoint promotion. No checkpoint rejection as a strength decision. No torch.load. No checkpoint blob loading. No live SC2. No GPU inference. No XAI execution. No human-panel evaluation. No showcase release. No v2 authorization. No T2–T5 execution. No raw out/, replay, video, checkpoint, or private operator evidence committed.

**Provisional next:** **`§V15-M57`** — *Governed Evaluation Execution Charter / Dry-Run Gate* (**provisional**; consumes sealed **§V15-M56** readout; freezes what governed evaluation execution means before benchmark/pass/fail claims — **not** benchmark execution, promotion, **`torch.load`**, live SC2, GPU inference, XAI, human-panel, showcase, **v2**, or **T2–T5** unless explicitly chartered).

**M50 upstream caveat (preserved):** **M50** upstream remains **`fixture_ci`** bounded posture. The **M53** chain proves governed operator wiring, Phase A live adapter smoke, and 12-hour training execution. It does **not** convert **M50**/**M49** scorecard fields into benchmark pass/fail evidence.

### V15-M18 — Candidate Checkpoint Evaluation Readiness & Refusal Contract

V15-M18 defines when candidate checkpoint evaluation may begin and when STARLAB must refuse to infer strength. It preserves the M17 posture that watchability, sandbox behavior, `.joblib` harness plumbing, and `not_executed` long-GPU receipts are not promoted checkpoint evidence. **`candidate_ready_for_evaluation`** is **ready_for_future_evaluation** only (input contract), not a benchmark result.

**Public closeout (2026-04-27):** [PR #150](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/150); merge `e58e249e85ed2a25d521783818104473bbd8e2bd`; authoritative PR-head [`25023439537`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25023439537) (head `9fae3273…`); merge-boundary `main` [`25023582158`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25023582158) — **success**.

### V15-M19 — Candidate checkpoint evaluation **package** assembly (closed)

M18 is the **readiness** gate; **M19** is the **package assembly** gate. M19 copies an audit-useful M18 summary, binds the full M18 JSON by **SHA-256**, and **independently** checks consistency of checkpoint-related hashes across candidate manifest, M03 lineage, M08 receipt, and the M18 snapshot — **without** hashing raw checkpoint blobs. The default **evaluation protocol** bind is the **M05** strong-agent scorecard JSON (`v15_strong_agent_scorecard.json`, `contract_id` **`starlab.v15.strong_agent_scorecard.v1`**, `protocol_profile_id` **`starlab.v15.strong_agent_benchmark_protocol.v1`**). Gates **P0–P9** in the checklist cover readiness binding, inputs, lineage, environment, dataset, protocol, cross-SHA consistency, public/private boundary, and **M20** fork recommendation.

**Public closeout (2026-04-27):** [PR #151](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/151); merge `e9a40a21fd10a454b1f26fcbccac28e487fab4ee`; authoritative PR-head [`25025083247`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25025083247) (head `4ec72325…`); merge-boundary `main` [`25025427887`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25025427887) on merge `e9a40a21…` — **success**. Default public fixture: **`blocked_missing_candidate_checkpoint_evidence`**; **`evaluation_package_ready`** = **`ready_for_future_checkpoint_evaluation` only** when emitted under aligned governed inputs.

- Assembly-only **`evaluation_package_ready`** does **not** authorize XAI, human-benchmark, showcase, or v2 work; those tracks remain **M20+** as governed in **`docs/starlab-v1.5.md`**.

### V15-M20 — Real Candidate Checkpoint Production Gate

V15-M20 closed with tooling, fixture gate, and operator-local T1 run path implemented. The default public/CI posture remains **`fixture_no_operator_run`**; a private dry-run preflight passed, but the full operator-local T1 30-minute GPU run was not performed as part of merge CI. V15-M20 does not evaluate strength, promote a checkpoint, run benchmark evaluation, execute XAI or human-panel work, authorize v2, or execute the 2-hour / 12-hour tiers.

**Contract:** `starlab.v15.real_candidate_checkpoint_production_gate.v1` — **`docs/runtime/v15_real_candidate_checkpoint_production_gate_v1.md`** — **`python -m starlab.v15.emit_v15_real_candidate_checkpoint_production_gate`** — **`python -m starlab.v15.run_v15_t1_30min_candidate_checkpoint_gate`** (operator-local orchestrator).

**Public posture (default fixture / CI):** **`fixture_no_operator_run`** unless an operator-local run records honest artifacts under **`out/`** with explicit guards.

**Non-claims:** **`not_strength_evaluation`**, **`not_checkpoint_promotion`**, **`not_benchmark_pass`**, **`not_xai_execution`**, **`not_human_benchmark_execution`**, **`not_showcase_release`**, **`not_v2_authorization`**, **`not_2_hour_run`**, **`not_12_hour_run`** (enumerated on the gate JSON **`non_claims`** field).

### V15-M22 — Real Operator T1 30-Minute GPU Run Attempt & Evidence Capture

**V15-M22** — **closed** on `main` ([PR #154](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/154); merge `364ce5b65a04f724b88fd8ac91d15ab91586ba44` merged **2026-04-28T03:08:37Z** UTC). **Authoritative PR-head CI** [`25031597888`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25031597888) (head `ad0191fb4bd388bb979addd8ee5728680165f151`); **merge-boundary `main` CI** [`25031726394`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25031726394) on merge commit `364ce5b6…` — **success**. **M22** attempted the real operator-local **T1** path per program discipline; execution **did not** reach **`run_v15_m21_t1_30min_gpu_run_execution`** because minimum launch criteria failed first: **`torch_cuda_unavailable`** (active Python imported **CPU-only** PyTorch). **Classification:** **`operator_preflight_blocked`**. **Strongest allowed claim:** STARLAB attempted the real **T1** execution posture under **M22**, but governed preflight blocked on **torch_cuda_unavailable**. **V15-M23** **closed** the environment blocker on `main` ([PR #156](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/156); **§V15-M23** below). **V15-M24** **closed** on `main` ([PR #159](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/159); **§V15-M24** below) — **`operator_preflight_blocked` / `missing_private_manifest_inputs`**.

### V15-M23 — CUDA PyTorch Operator Environment Remediation

**V15-M23** — **closed** on `main` ([PR #156](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/156); merge `7ceb750a011de9a4ae4b33b9f7d46e81420dc009` merged **2026-04-28T04:00:06Z** UTC). **Authoritative PR-head CI** [`25032909816`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25032909816) (head `6268575aff9272b099a6c65ffac832ae327c5e54`); **merge-boundary `main` CI** [`25033137726`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25033137726) on merge commit `7ceb750a…` — **success**. **Public program / ledger alignment** on `main` ([PR #157](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/157); **authoritative PR-head CI** [`25033845338`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25033845338) (head `8c437098171b1242e871f24c4f4948c1556e3811`); **merge-boundary `main` CI** [`25033954220`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25033954220) on merge `e43d0def…` — **success**). **M23 public closeout (operator-local posture):** repo **`.venv`** carries CUDA-enabled **PyTorch** (**`torch 2.11.0+cu128`**, CUDA **12.8**); **`torch.cuda.is_available()`** **true**; GPU **NVIDIA GeForce RTX 5090**; simple CUDA tensor succeeded. Default **PATH** **Python** remains **CPU-only** and **must not** be used for STARLAB **GPU** runs — use **`./.venv/Scripts/python.exe`** (Windows) or an activated **`.venv`**. **M21** dry-run preflight was **not** rerun in **M23** (private manifest paths **not** supplied on the public record). **No** real **T1** / checkpoint / strength / benchmark / XAI / human / showcase / **v2** / **T2**/**T3** claims. Branch `v15-m23-cuda-pytorch-operator-env-remediation` was the implementation line. **V15-M24** **closed** on `main` ([PR #159](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/159); PR-head [`25036985830`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25036985830); merge-boundary [`25037125881`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25037125881)) recording operator-local **`operator_preflight_blocked` / `missing_private_manifest_inputs`** — `.venv` CUDA re-verified; **M21** **not** invoked (no on-disk **V15-M15** preflight JSON); see **§Status** paragraph and **§V15-M24**. **V15-M25** (**§V15-M25**) records **M15** JSON + **M21** dry-run alignment.

### V15-M24 — Real Operator T1 30-Minute GPU Run Attempt & Evidence Capture (operator-local record)

### V15-M26 — Real Operator T1 30-Minute GPU Run Attempt After Manifest Alignment

Implementation branch: `v15-m26-real-t1-30min-gpu-run` (governance PR [PR #162](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/162)).

**Public narrative (required):** M26 completed T1 checkpoint-production plumbing and produced a candidate checkpoint via synthetic CUDA, but the SC2 rollout path remained bounded smoke/bootstrap only and is not yet meaningful SC2 training.

**Required distinction (do not conflate paths):**

1. **Attempt A — SC2/bootstrap path (`local_live_sc2`):** one governed **M50** bootstrap episode on the **pass1b** line; **no** PyTorch training loop in that plan slice when **`max_training_steps`:** **0**; **not** acceptable as clean bounded **T1** or as evidence of **meaningful SC2 training**.
2. **Attempt B — `t1_synthetic_cuda_training` path:** bounded **PyTorch CUDA** **MLP** training **after** bootstrap; produces a **candidate** **`.pt`** and honest hash — **useful checkpoint-production plumbing** on the **synthetic T1 surface**; **not** evidence of **SC2 gameplay learning**; **not** strength, benchmark, XAI, human-panel, showcase, or **v2**.

**SC2/bootstrap investigation (why an observed match can look trivially short):**

- Representative operator-local artifact: **`match_execution_proof.json`** under **`.../phases/pass1b_live_sc2_bootstrap/episodes/e000/`** (paths vary by **`execution_id`**).
- Default **BurnySC2** harness (non–PX1-hybrid / non-watchability policy) uses an internal **`_HarnessBot`** that **does not** drive macro/micro learning — it records observations and issues **`bounded_exit`** / **`client.leave()`** after **`bounded_horizon.max_game_steps`** iterations (`starlab/sc2/adapters/burnysc2_adapter.py`). **`step_policy`** in proofs typically records **`game_step`** and **`max_game_steps`** (e.g. **128** steps); **`action_count`** may remain **zero**; **`status_sequence`** includes **`bounded_exit`**; **`sc2_game_result`** may read **`Defeat`** after voluntary leave — **not** the same as a sustained ladder-quality match.
- **Game end:** controlled **bounded horizon** / harness exit — **not** necessarily crash-only; wall-clock can be **very short** even when in-game loops advance (fast headless stepping).
- **Training:** **`max_training_steps`:** **0** on Attempt A plan removes any manifest-claimed PyTorch trainer cadence for that attempt; **M26** routing runs **SC2** bootstrap then (Attempt B) **synthetic CUDA** — SC2 is **smoke / bootstrap**, not the **MLP** learner.

**M26 acceptance standard (user / program intent):** M26 **does not** close as “successful **SC2** **T1**” on **`main`** unless one holds: **(a)** a **real SC2-backed** training or rollout workload that is **materially non-trivial** (not harness-only smoke), **or** **(b)** multiple meaningful rollout episodes with **nonzero** training/update steps tied to SC2 execution, **or** **(c)** a **documented concrete blocker** why the current **SC2** runner cannot yet sustain that posture. **Synthetic CUDA alone** does **not** satisfy that **SC2** bar.

**Attempt A — pass1b-only (`out/v15_m26/t1_real_attempt`, intermediate):** **`python -m starlab.v15.run_v15_m21_t1_30min_gpu_run_execution`** with **`--allow-operator-local-execution`**, **`--authorize-t1-30min-gpu-run`**, **`--max-wall-clock-minutes`:** **30**, M25-aligned manifest argv, and **without** **`--dry-run-preflight-only`**. First launch **exit 4** — **`sc2`** import until **`pip install -e ".[sc2-harness]"`** into **`.venv`**. Second launch: M08 **exit 0**; one **`local_live_sc2`** bootstrap episode; plan **`max_training_steps`:** **0** — **no** PyTorch training loop; ~**16 s** wall-clock; **M20/M21** **`t1_30min_run_completed_no_checkpoint`** / **`no_pytorch_checkpoint_artifact_under_execution_root`**. **Historic label:** **`t1_30min_completed_without_candidate_checkpoint`** (Attempt A only).

**Attempt B — emitted M26 campaign (`out/v15_m26/t1_campaign_plan/`) + `t1_synthetic_cuda_training`:** after M50 bootstrap, when **`run_tier`:** **`T1_30_MIN`**, executor runs bounded **PyTorch CUDA** MLP training (protocol phase kind **`t1_synthetic_cuda_training`**; default **`min_wall_seconds`:** **300**; override **`STARLAB_T1_SYNTHETIC_CUDA_MIN_WALL_SECONDS`** for shorter iteration). **M20** rejects sub-**300 s** no-checkpoint completions (**`t1_30min_run_failed_insufficient_training_workload`**, exit **9**). Checkpoints under **`campaign_runs/<execution_id>/`** (discovery vs legacy **`m08_campaign_execution`** tree).

**Validated operator-local attempt (`out/v15_m26/t1_real_attempt_004`):** **M20** **`gate_status`:** **`t1_30min_checkpoint_produced_package_ready`**; **candidate** **`.pt`** **SHA-256** **`cb375b77a92f6f07b406d8579a60f3539568be12877808d600826c049e146e78`** — **candidate produced by synthetic CUDA T1 training surface** (**candidate only**, **no** promotion). **~135 s** observed with **`STARLAB_T1_SYNTHETIC_CUDA_MIN_WALL_SECONDS=120`** (production-shaped default is **≥300 s** synthetic wall or earlier checkpoint per protocol). **SC2/bootstrap gameplay remained trivial / harness-bounded** for this milestone line — **not meaningful SC2 agent training yet**.

**Program outcome note:** **`t1_30min_completed_with_candidate_checkpoint`** (documentation vocabulary) aligns with **`t1_30min_checkpoint_produced_package_ready`** + hash-recorded **`.pt`** — **plumbing / packaging** posture; **not** a **SC2** strength result; **not** promotion. **Evidence classification (narrative):** **`t1_checkpoint_plumbing_completed_but_sc2_training_not_yet_meaningful`**.

**Public governance:** **closed** on `main` ([PR #162](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/162); merge `393adb7fb91536c16927b93216bc7045981061e5` merged **2026-04-28T10:15:38Z** UTC). **Authoritative PR-head CI** [`25046959088`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25046959088) (head `9d877da21bd94df1d0685215ca9f29aac808ac98`); **merge-boundary `main` CI** [`25047132158`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25047132158) on merge commit `393adb7f…` — **success**. **Honest closeout:** **checkpoint plumbing** + **SC2 integration gap** — **do not** reframe as **successful SC2 T1 training**; **synthetic CUDA** **≠** **meaningful SC2 agent training**.

### V15-M28 — SC2-Backed T1 Candidate Training Attempt

**Distinction vs M26/M27:** **M26** proved **synthetic CUDA** checkpoint plumbing without meaningful **SC2** training; **M27** proved **SC2** rollout + integration-smoke binding (**not** candidate-training strength). **V15-M28** is the first bounded **SC2-backed** **T1 candidate-training** attempt that **reads governed M27 rollout fields**, derives a **feature vector**, and performs **PyTorch** updates **conditioned** on that vector (**`sc2_rollout_feature_conditioned_training_smoke_not_strength_learning`** — **not** ladder competence).

**Public closeout (2026-04-28):** [PR #164](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/pull/164); merge `35d59f11e64b5b8fcb2c2937572478bfa9f37863` merged **2026-04-28T23:40:35Z** UTC; authoritative PR-head [`25083196925`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25083196925) (head `40550e6481c6f5988cd72e210e2a17d16f533e81`); merge-boundary `main` [`25083354466`](https://github.com/m-cahill/starlab/actions/runs/25083354466) — **success**.

**Contract:** **`starlab.v15.sc2_backed_t1_candidate_training.v1`** — **`docs/runtime/v15_sc2_backed_t1_candidate_training_v1.md`** — **`python -m starlab.v15.run_v15_m28_sc2_backed_t1_candidate_training`**.

**Upstream M27 bind:** canonical **`artifact_sha256`** over **`out/v15_m27/sc2_rollout_integration_run1/v15_sc2_rollout_training_loop_integration.json`** (**`f9c2ca5aca7a3b15df0567358c1f207f99e112cd8d816f5ac1a1c6ff04022227`** — verification uses **canonical JSON seal**, not raw file digest).

**Operator-local evidence (dual-guard path; default merge CI: `--fixture-only` → `fixture_only`):**

- **`sc2_backed_features_used`:** **true** when episodes + tallies feed the feature tensor.
- **`m28_outcome` (operator-local sample):** **`sc2_backed_candidate_training_completed_with_candidate_checkpoint`**.
- **Training updates observed (sample):** **170** — **bounded smoke** permits early stop (**`max_training_updates`**, **loss-floor**, **`wall_clock_budget`**) unless operator uses **`--require-full-wall-clock`** / aligned flags — **not** standalone proof operator execution consumed **`~≥1800` seconds**.
- **Candidate checkpoint `.pt` SHA-256 (sample, final cadence-bound artifact):** **`71897cfff94fba7209e667dd44e040eabc705e686c6a579cd26e13015f00ecc8`** (**candidate only**, **no promotion**).
- **Sealed M28 JSON SHA-256 (sample operator emit):** **`3d73fad35fb4af0273272d03b5eace6131de4346e2ad645270edc970a1821e79`** — **local `out/v15_m28/**` — **not committed**.
- **`m20_m21_gate_integration`:** **`m20_m21_candidate_gate_integration_deferred_to_m30`** (non-blocking).

**Fixture CI:** **`fixture_only`** — **no** upstream M27 path required; **no** live **SC2** in CI.

### V15-M29 — Full 30-minute SC2-backed T1 candidate run & evaluation package gate

**Distinction vs M28:** **M28** can exit early (**loss floor**, **`max_updates`**, **`wall_clock_budget`**) unless operator enables **explicit full-horizon training flags**. **M29** records whether operator-local execution satisfies **`observed_wall_clock_seconds`** against the configured **`requested_min_wall_clock_seconds`** (**default target ~1800s**, **±bounded tolerance** on classification paths) via **`starlab.v15.full_30min_sc2_backed_t1_run.v1`** (`python -m starlab.v15.run_v15_m29_full_30min_sc2_backed_t1_run`) — **delegates** to **`run_v15_m28_sc2_backed_t1_candidate_training`** with **opt-in** `--require-full-wall-clock` semantics by default through the wrapper.

**Package / operator readiness:** merge CI **`fixture_schema_only_no_operator_package`**; honest operator success **`package_ready_for_future_candidate_evaluation`** (**structural** readiness for future bounded evaluation routing — **not** benchmark execution executed here).

**Binding fix (`ub_m39_expected` tuple):** Restoring intended tuple shape after a malformed 1-tuple from a trailing comma after a ternary fixes governed **manifest vs expected-receipt** alignment for sealed **M41**-derived expectations (**binding / routing bookkeeping** — **not** a change in evaluation semantics, benchmark interpretation, or strength posture).


**Authority:** sealed **M41** JSON is **mandatory** (`--m41-package-json`). Direct **M39** artifacts are **optional cross-checks** only — **no** normal success path bypasses M41.

**M42 non-claims block:** **not** benchmark matches; **not** strength evaluation; **not** checkpoint promotion; **not** scorecard **results**; **not** **`torch.load`** / checkpoint blob loading; **not** live SC2 in this packaging surface; **not** XAI; **not** human-panel; **not** showcase; **not** **v2**; **not** **T2**/**T3**.

**Strongest allowed claim (M42):** **V15-M42** assembles/routes a governed candidate-checkpoint evaluation package from the validated **V15-M41** package and consistent candidate/receipt bindings, making the final two-hour candidate **structurally** ready for **future bounded evaluation routing** (**not** execution of that routing here).

V15-M42 does **not** execute benchmark matches, evaluate strength, promote checkpoints, produce scorecard **results**, invoke **`torch.load`**, load checkpoint blobs, run live SC2, run XAI, run human-panel evaluation, release a showcase agent, authorize **v2**, or execute **T2**/**T3**.

**M43 non-claims:** **not** benchmark execution; **not** benchmark outcome / strength / promotion claims; **not** **`torch.load`** or checkpoint blobs; **not** scorecard results; **not** live SC2 / XAI / human panel / showcase / **v2** / **T2**/**T3**/**T4**/**T5** execution here — **V15-M43 does not authorize benchmark execution**.

### V15-M02 — Environment lock status (compact)

Fixture CI proves **wiring and schema**; **operator-local** evidence is required to claim a real **Gate B** environment. Default operator-local status is **`not_evaluated`** until a probe is recorded.

| Environment surface | Required evidence (operator) | CI fixture | Operator-local (default) | Public / private | Next |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Repo identity | git SHA, branch, repo | `fixture` (stable placeholders) | `not_evaluated` | public-safe SHAs; no unsanitized paths | **M03+** |
| Python | version, platform, venv policy | `fixture` | `not_evaluated` | public | ongoing |
| Dependency lock / hash | fingerprint, lockfile refs | `fixture` | `not_evaluated` | public refs; private local paths | ongoing |
| CUDA | version, driver posture | not evaluated in fixture | `not_evaluated` | mostly **private_local_only** in notes | **M07**+ |
| PyTorch | torch build, CUDA build string | not evaluated in fixture | `not_evaluated` | public versions | **M07**+ |
| GPU | name, mem, driver | not evaluated in fixture | `not_evaluated` | private by default (sanitize for public) | **M07**+ |
| SC2 client | version, declared path posture | not evaluated in fixture | `not_evaluated` | **Blizzard TOS**; path **private** | **M07**+ |
| Map pool | pool id, required map list | not evaluated in fixture | `not_evaluated` | logical refs; raw paths **private** | **C** / **M07**+ |
| Disk / output root | policy, min free space | not evaluated in fixture | `not_evaluated` | **private** absolute roots | **M08**+ |
| Operator notes | optional text | N/A in fixture | optional | `private_local_only` by default | ongoing |

`long_gpu_run_authorized` in the M02 contract is **always false**; use **`operator_local_ready`** (with `--probe-json`) for “M02 check list satisfied,” not for program go-ahead.

### V15-M03 — Checkpoint lineage status (compact)

| Checkpoint surface | What M03 defines | Fixture (`fixture_ci`) | Operator-local (typical) | Public / private posture | Next dependent milestone |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Checkpoint identity** | `checkpoint_id`, roles, URI/ref | `fixture-root`, `fixture-child` (metadata only) | `not_evaluated` until declared | logical refs; paths **redacted** / **private** as needed | M07+ (shakedown) / M08+ |
| **Parent/child lineage** | `parent_checkpoint_id` graph | `fixture` chain | `not_evaluated` / declared in lineage JSON | public-safe if no paths leaked | M08+ |
| **Checkpoint hash reference** | `checkpoint_sha256` + `hash_verification_status` | all-zero placeholder; `fixture` status | `declared_only` / `verified_external` (pass-through) | hash refs public; **blobs** private | M09+ promotion |
| **Model config binding** | `model_config_sha256` per row + ref | placeholder | `not_evaluated` / declared | public refs; private paths | M08+ |
| **Dataset / register binding** | `dataset_manifest_sha256` + manifest refs | placeholder | `not_evaluated` / declared | public refs; private corpora | Gate **C** / M08+ |
| **Environment lock binding** | `environment_lock_sha256` + optional M02 file bind | not bound to a real M02 file | `not_evaluated` / `--environment-lock-json` | public SHA only; no unsanitized paths | M02 evidence + M08+ |
| **Interruption receipt** | `interruption_receipts[]` | fixture-shaped | operator-declared / external attestation (not verified by M03) | sanitize paths | M08+ |
| **Resume receipt** | `resume_receipts[]` | `resume_verification_status` may be `fixture` (not execution) | `declared_only` / `not_executed` default | same | M07+ proves execution |
| **Rollback receipt** | `rollback_receipts[]` | `fixture` (not execution) | `declared_only` / `not_executed` default | same | M09+ |
| **Promotion status** | `promotion_status` + vocabulary | `fixture_only` for fixture rows | candidate / … per gate | public narrative only w/ non-claims | M09+ |

`checkpoint_bytes_verified` is **true** only if **every** checkpoint row has `hash_verification_status == "verified_external"` (operator pass-through; M03 does not read blobs). `resume_execution_verified` and `rollback_execution_verified` are **false** in M03. `long_gpu_run_authorized` is **false**.

### V15-M05 — Strong-agent benchmark status (compact)

M05 separates **protocol defined** (CI fixture + optional operator declaration), **benchmark executed** (real matches / evaluation), and **strong-agent claim authorized** (program-level certification) — the latter two remain **false** in M05.

| Benchmark surface | What M05 defines | Fixture protocol exists | Benchmark executed | Strong-agent claim authorized | Public / private posture | Next dependent milestone |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `evaluation_ladder` | E0–E8 stage ids, names, `stage_status` vocabulary | yes / fixture + vocabulary | false | false | public-safe; no unsanitized paths | **M09+** / eval execution |
| `protocol_profile` | `starlab.v15.strong_agent_benchmark_protocol.v1` | yes / metadata | n/a (not an execution) | false | public | **M09+** |
| `candidate_identity` | Candidate + baseline **subject** row shapes; fixture ids | yes / fixture | false | false | logical refs; paths **redacted** | M03+ bind / **M09+** |
| `checkpoint_binding` | SHA references only (no blob reads in M05) | fixture placeholder | false | false | hash refs public | M03+ / **M08+** |
| `map_pool` | Map pool + rights posture **shape** | yes / fixture | false | false | logical map ids; raw paths private | **M07+** / gate **C** |
| `opponent_pool` | Opponent pool **shape** | yes / fixture | false | false | public-safe ids in fixture | **M09+** |
| `scorecard_fields` | Required metric **names** / field definitions (no results) | yes / all required metrics listed | false | false | public vocabulary | **M09+** |
| `gate_thresholds` | Gate / threshold **definitions** (no pass/fail outcome) | yes / fixture | false | false | public protocol text | **M09+** |
| `evidence_requirements` | Required evidence **kinds** (M02/M03/M04 contracts) | yes / fixture | false | false | public contract refs | M02–M04 bind / **M10** |
| `failure_mode_probes` | Probe **schema** (not executed) | yes / fixture | false | false | public-safe | **M09+** |
| `xai_trace_requirements` | XAI pack trace coverage as **requirement** only | yes / defined | false | false | public | **M10+** (review) |
| `human_panel_reserved` | **Reserved** for **V15-M06+**; `reserved`, `claim_authorized` false | yes / section present | false | false | public narrative; participants private | **M06+** |
| `xai_review_reserved` | **Reserved** for **V15-M10+**; `review_performed` / `faithfulness_validated` false | yes / section present | false | false | public | **M10+** |

`long_gpu_run_authorized`, `benchmark_execution_performed`, and `strong_agent_claim_authorized` in the M05 scorecard contract are **always false** in M05 (fixture or operator-declared **protocol** path).

### V15-M06 — Human panel benchmark status (compact)

M06 separates **protocol defined** (CI fixture + optional operator **declaration**), **human panel executed** (real / operator-local **matches** in a later milestone), and **human benchmark claim authorized** (program-level certification) — the latter two remain **false** in M06.

| Human-panel surface | What M06 defines | Fixture protocol exists | Human panel executed | Human benchmark claim authorized | Public / private posture | Next dependent milestone |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `participant_tiers` | Deterministic `tier_id` vocabulary | yes / fixture | false | false | public-safe; no real roster in fixture | **M11+** |
| `participant_privacy_profile` | Strict `posture_id` enum rows | yes / fixture | false | false | public vocabulary; rosters private | **M11+** |
| `threshold_policy` | Majority / supermajority / tier / freeze **options** | yes / no pass/fail | false | false | public protocol text | **M11+** |
| `evidence_requirements` | Required evidence **kinds** (not filled results) | yes / classes | false | false | public contract refs | M02–M05 bind / **M11** |
| `claim_boundary` | Allowed + disallowed **claim** shapes (text) | yes / fixture | false | false | public | **M11+** |
| `optional_bindings` | SHA-256 of M02 / M03 / M05 / M04 **JSON** only | optional | n/a | false | public SHA; no path leaks in operator path | M02–M05 |

`benchmark_execution_performed`, `human_panel_execution_performed`, `human_benchmark_claim_authorized`, `strong_agent_claim_authorized`, and `long_gpu_run_authorized` in the M06 contract are **false** in M06 (fixture or operator-**declared** **protocol** path).

---

## 6. Artifact family contract ids (governed names)

These are the **intended** v1.5 contract identifiers (emission implemented per milestone; M00 defines names and charter JSON).

- `starlab.v15.training_readiness_charter.v1` (**M00**)
- `starlab.v15.training_asset_registers.v1` (**M01** — register contract / vocabulary only)
- `starlab.v15.long_gpu_environment_lock.v1` (**M02** — environment-lock contract; fixture and optional operator probe)
- `starlab.v15.long_gpu_training_manifest.v1` (**M08** — long campaign manifest + preflight; `starlab.v15.long_gpu_campaign_receipt.v1` for operator-local receipt stub)
- `starlab.v15.checkpoint_lineage_manifest.v1` (**M03** — checkpoint lineage + receipt vocabulary; **implemented** in M03; **not** a training or checkpoint I/O **runtime**)
- `starlab.v15.training_run_receipt.v1` (**M07** — training smoke / shakedown receipt; **not** long campaign)
- `starlab.v15.strong_agent_scorecard.v1` (**M05** — strong-agent scorecard / benchmark **protocol** contract; **not** executed benchmark; embeds **`protocol_profile_id`:** `starlab.v15.strong_agent_benchmark_protocol.v1`)
- `starlab.v15.xai_evidence_pack.v1` (**M04** — XAI pack contract; **implemented** in M04; **not** real XAI inference)
- `starlab.v15.human_panel_benchmark.v1` (**M06** — human-panel **protocol** contract; **closed**; embeds **`protocol_profile_id`:** `starlab.v15.human_panel_benchmark_protocol.v1`)
- `starlab.v15.checkpoint_evaluation.v1` (**M09** — checkpoint **evaluation** contract; **not** verified blob evaluation in fixture CI)
- `starlab.v15.checkpoint_promotion_decision.v1` (**M09** — promotion **decision** contract; **not** strong-agent claim)
- `starlab.v15.replay_native_xai_demonstration.v1` (**M10** — XAI **demonstration/reporting** surface; **binds** M04/M09 JSON by SHA; **not** inference)
- `starlab.v15.human_panel_execution.v1` (**M11** — human-panel **execution** metadata + H0–H12 **gates**; **binds** M06/M09/M10 JSON by SHA; **not** real panel execution in CI)
- `starlab.v15.human_benchmark_claim_decision.v1` (**M11** — **claim decision** over execution JSON; **not** a second upstream binder)
- `starlab.v15.showcase_agent_release_pack.v1`
- `starlab.v15.v2_go_no_go_decision.v1` (**M13** — v2 **decision** surface only; **not** v2 implementation)
- `starlab.v15.v2_decision_operator_evidence_declared.v1` (**M13** — optional operator metadata; **not** proof of execution)
- `starlab.v15.evidence_remediation_plan.v1` (**M14** — evidence-gap inventory and remediation plan; **not** operator execution; **not** v2 authorization)
- `starlab.v15.operator_evidence_collection_preflight.v1` (**M15** — operator evidence **preflight** and sequencing; **not** collection; **not** v2)
- `starlab.v15.short_gpu_environment_evidence.v1` (**M16** — bounded environment / short-GPU evidence; **not** long campaign; **`long_gpu_run_authorized` false**)
- `starlab.v15.long_gpu_campaign_evidence.v1` (**M17** — long GPU campaign **evidence / preflight** wrapper; **not** a substitute for M08 execution receipts unless operator-run; **`long_gpu_run_authorized` false** on default paths)
- `starlab.v15.checkpoint_evaluation_readiness.v1` (**M18** — candidate checkpoint **readiness / refusal** only; **not** evaluation execution; **not** strength)
- `starlab.v15.candidate_checkpoint_manifest.v1` (**M18** — optional logical manifest shape for operator-supplied inputs; **metadata only**)
- `starlab.v15.real_candidate_checkpoint_production_gate.v1` (**M20** — T1 checkpoint-production **gate** vocabulary + orchestrator wiring)
- `starlab.v15.operator_t1_30min_gpu_run_execution.v1` (**M21** — operator **T1** execution / evidence framing; delegates training path to **M20** orchestrator)
- `starlab.v15.sc2_rollout_training_loop_integration.v1` (**M27** — SC2 rollout + integration-smoke training binding receipts)
- `starlab.v15.sc2_backed_t1_candidate_training.v1` (**M28** — SC2 rollout features → bounded PyTorch trainer; **`long_gpu_run_authorized`** false unless separately evidenced)
- `starlab.v15.full_30min_sc2_backed_t1_run.v1` (**M29** — full-wall-clock SC2-backed T1 candidate-training receipts wrapper; binds M27/M28 SHAs **without strength/benchmark promotion claims**)

---

## 7. Long GPU run gate (definition)

Training at “long GPU run” scale is **not** treated as program-valid until gates **A–G** are explicitly satisfied by evidence in later milestones. Summary:

| Gate | Name | Intent |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **A** | Governance | Charter, claims, non-claims, public/private surfaces |
| **B** | Environment | GPU, CUDA/PyTorch, SC2, maps, disk, dependency pins |
| **C** | Data | Manifests, hashes, rights, reproducible labels |
| **D** | Checkpoints | Hashing, lineage, resume, rollback, promotion states |
| **E** | Evaluation | Frozen scorecard / baselines, fixture and live paths as declared |
| **F** | XAI | Frozen contract, fixture pack, traces, reports |
| **G** | Operator | Runbook, stop/resume, retention, failure handling |

Canonical machine-readable structure: `long_gpu_run_gates` in `v15_training_readiness_charter.json`.

---

## 8. Evaluation ladder (summary)

Ordered evidence stages used for v1.5 evaluation narrative (details in moonshot doc): **E0** artifact integrity → **E1** fixture smoke → **E2** scripted baselines → **E3** heuristic baselines → **E4** prior STARLAB checkpoints → **E5** local live SC2 (bounded) → **E6** exploit/failure probes → **E7** human panel → **E8** XAI review.

---

## 9. XAI demonstration surfaces (minimum)

Minimum demonstration expectations include governance-style artifacts such as: decision trace, attribution / concept summaries, counterfactual probes, alternative action rankings, replay overlay manifest, and an explanation report—bound to replay and checkpoint identity. **M00** defines intent; later milestones freeze formats and emit fixture packs.

---

## 10. Configuration and reproducibility governance

Long runs must bind identity and environment fields (git SHA, branch, milestone, Python/deps, CUDA, PyTorch, GPU, SC2 version, map pool, seeds, dataset and checkpoint hashes, config hash, operator notes). Run-class manifests (training, environment, hardware, dataset, checkpoint, evaluation, XAI, human benchmark, rights) are expected for v1.5-scale evidence. **M00** states the requirement; **V15-M01+** implements registers and automation as needed.

---

## 11. CI security note (M00–M07, temporary)

The default merge CI runs **`pip-audit`** with a **single** narrow ignore: **`--ignore-vuln CVE-2026-3219`** for the **`pip` toolchain**. **M01 re-check (2026-04-24, CI-like env):** after `pip install --upgrade pip`, **`pip` 26.0.1** still reported **CVE-2026-3219** to **`pip-audit`**. **M02 re-check (2026-04-25, CI-like local env):** same — **`pip` 26.0.1** still reports the CVE; **no** audit-clean **`pip`** upgrade path observed. **M03 re-check (2026-04-25, local env):** **`pip` 26.0.1** is still the latest on PyPI; **`pip-audit`** still flags **CVE-2026-3219** for **`pip`**. **M04 re-check (2026-04-25, local env):** **`pip index versions pip`** still shows **26.0.1** as latest; **no** newer audit-clean wheel observed — **leave** the **same** single narrow ignore. **M05 re-check (2026-04-25, local env):** **`pip index versions pip`** still shows **26.0.1** as latest; **no** audit-clean fixed **`pip`** on PyPI observed — **leave** the same single narrow ignore; do **not** broaden exceptions. **M06 re-check (2026-04-25, local env):** **`python -m pip index versions pip`** still shows **26.0.1** as **LATEST**; **no** newer audit-clean **`pip`** on PyPI observed — **leave** the same single narrow **pip-only** ignore; do **not** broaden exceptions. **M07 re-check (2026-04-25, local env):** same — **`pip` 26.0.1** still latest; **leave** the **same** narrow **`pip`**-only **CVE-2026-3219** ignore; do **not** broaden. This is **not** `continue-on-error`. **CycloneDX SBOM** generation, **SBOM upload**, **Gitleaks**, and the aggregate **governance** job still run. **Remove** the ignore when a fixed, audit-clean **`pip`** is published on PyPI.

---

## 12. Open risks and carry-forward items (M32-family)

Addressed or explicitly deferred in future **V15** milestones:

- Meaningful **coverage** gate vs floor-only policy.
- **CI tiering** (fast / slow / operator-local) vs default merge path truthfulness.
- **JSON I/O** deduplication at long-run scale.
- **Architecture** overview for training-scale operator paths.
- **Provenance** for replay, data, weights, and benchmarks under long-run storage.

---

## 13. Document maintenance (per `.cursorrules`)

Any milestone that changes artifact shape, contract behavior, interface boundaries, environment pins, or replay/evaluation semantics must update **this file** in the same milestone. This document must stay synchronized with code, label **stable vs provisional** surfaces, and remain suitable as the first document an auditor reads for v1.5.
